#### <a name="what-about-bluetooth-microphone-support&quot;></a><span data-ttu-id=&quot;39c90-481&quot;>蓝牙麦克风支持呢？</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;39c90-481&quot;>What about Bluetooth microphone support?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id=&quot;39c90-482&quot;>遗憾的是，蓝牙麦克风目前仍不受 HoloLens 2。</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;39c90-482&quot;>Unfortunately Bluetooth microphones are still not currently supported on HoloLens 2.</span></span>

#### <a name=&quot;troubleshooting-usb-c-microphones&quot;></a><span data-ttu-id=&quot;39c90-483&quot;>USB-C 麦克风疑难解答</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;39c90-483&quot;>Troubleshooting USB-C microphones</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id=&quot;39c90-484&quot;>请注意，某些 USB-C 麦克风错误地将自身报告为 *麦克风和扬声器* 。</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;39c90-484&quot;>Be aware that some USB-C microphones incorrectly report themselves as both a microphone *and* a speaker.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id=&quot;39c90-485&quot;>这是麦克风的问题，而不是 HoloLens 的问题。</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;39c90-485&quot;>This is a problem with the microphone and not with HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id=&quot;39c90-486&quot;>将其中一个麦克风插入 HoloLens 时，可能会丢失声音。</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;39c90-486&quot;>When plugging one of these microphones into HoloLens, sound may be lost.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id=&quot;39c90-487&quot;>幸运的是，有一个简单的修复方法。</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;39c90-487&quot;>Fortunately there is a simple fix.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id=&quot;39c90-488&quot;>在 **&quot;**  ->  **设置系统** 声音 (&quot;中，将&quot;模拟功能音频驱动程序") 将内置扬声器设置为  ->  **"默认设备"。** </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-488">In **Settings** -> **System** -> **Sound**, explicitly set the built-in speakers **(Analog Feature Audio Driver)** as the **Default device**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-489">即使稍后删除了麦克风并重新连接，HoloLens 也应记住此设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-489">HoloLens should remember this setting even if the microphone is removed and reconnected later.</span></span>

![USB-C 麦克风疑难解答](images/usbc-mic-4.png)

### <a name="visitor-auto-logon-for-kiosks"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-491">展台的访问者自动登录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-491">Visitor Auto logon for Kiosks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-492">此新功能使访问者帐户能够自动登录，以用于展台模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-492">This new feature enables the auto logon on Visitor accounts to be used for Kiosk modes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-493">对于非 AAD 配置，若要为访问者自动登录配置设备，</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-493">For a non-AAD configuration, to configure a device for visitor auto-logon:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-494">创建一个预配包，该包：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-494">Create a provisioning package that:</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-495">配置 **运行时设置/AssignedAccess** 以允许访问者帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-495">Configures **Runtime settings/AssignedAccess** to allow Visitor accounts.</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-496">（可选）将设备注册到 MDM (**运行时设置/工作区/** 注册) 以便以后可以管理该设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-496">Optionally enrolls the device in MDM **(Runtime settings/Workplace/Enrollments)** so that it can be managed later.</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-497">不创建本地帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-497">Do not create a local account</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-498">[应用预配包](hololens-provisioning.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-498">[Apply the provisioning package](hololens-provisioning.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-499">对于 AAD 配置，用户无需进行此更改即可实现与现在类似的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-499">For an AAD configuration, users can achieve something similar to this today without this change.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-500">为展台模式配置的已加入 AAD 的设备可以通过登录屏幕中的单个按钮点击来登录访问者帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-500">AAD joined devices configured for kiosk mode can sign in a Visitor account with a single button tap from the sign in screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-501">登录到访问者帐户后，在从 "开始" 菜单中显式注销访问者或重新启动设备之前，该设备将不会提示登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-501">Once signed in to the visitor account, the device will not prompt for sign in again until the Visitor is explicitly signed out from the start menu or the device is restarted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-502">可以通过 [自定义 OMA URI](https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/intune/configuration/custom-settings-windows-10) 策略来管理访问者自动登录：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-502">Visitor Auto logon can be managed via [custom OMA-URI](https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/intune/configuration/custom-settings-windows-10) policy:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-503">URI 值：./Device/Vendor/MSFT/MixedReality/VisitorAutoLogon</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-503">URI value: ./Device/Vendor/MSFT/MixedReality/VisitorAutoLogon</span></span>

### <a name="use-the-new-settings-and-edge-apps-in-kiosk-modes"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-510">在展台模式下使用新设置和边缘应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-510">Use the new Settings and Edge apps in Kiosk modes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-511">当在 [网亭](hololens-kiosk.md)中包含应用时，IT 管理员通常会将该应用添加到展台，但使用其应用用户模型 ID (AUMID) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-511">When including apps in [Kiosks](hololens-kiosk.md), an IT Admin often adds the app to the Kiosk but using it's App User Model ID (AUMID).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-512">由于 "设置" 应用和 Microsoft Edge 应用都被视为新应用，并且与将 AUMIDs 用于这些应用的较旧的应用网亭不同，因此需要将其更新为使用新的 AUMID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-512">Because both the Settings app and Microsoft Edge app are considered new apps and different than the older apps Kiosks that use AUMIDs for those apps will need to be updated to use the new AUMID.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-513">修改展台以包含新应用时，建议添加新的 AUMID，并保留旧的应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-513">When modifying a Kiosk to include the new apps, we recommend adding in the new AUMID as well as leaving the old one.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-514">这会在用户更新操作系统时创建轻松转换，而无需接收新策略，即可继续使用展台。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-514">This will create an easy transition when users update the OS and won't need to receive new policies to keep using the Kiosk as intended.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="39c90-515">应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-515">App</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="39c90-516">AUMID</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-516">AUMID</span></span>                                                  |
|------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="39c90-517">旧设置应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-517">Old Settings App</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="39c90-518">HolographicSystemSettings_cw5n1h2txyewy！应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-518">HolographicSystemSettings_cw5n1h2txyewy!App</span></span>            |
| <span data-ttu-id="39c90-519">新建设置应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-519">New Settings App</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="39c90-520">BAEAEF15-9BAB-47FC-ACECAD2AE94B_cw5n1h2txyewy 800B！应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-520">BAEAEF15-9BAB-47FC-800B-ACECAD2AE94B_cw5n1h2txyewy!App</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="39c90-521">旧的 Microsoft Edge 应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-521">Old Microsoft Edge app</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="39c90-522">Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge_8wekyb3d8bbwe!MicrosoftEdge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-522">Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge_8wekyb3d8bbwe!MicrosoftEdge</span></span>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="39c90-523">新的 Microsoft Edge 应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-523">New Microsoft Edge app</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="39c90-524">Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge.Stable_8wekyb3d8bbwe！MSEDGE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-524">Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge.Stable_8wekyb3d8bbwe!MSEDGE</span></span>    |

### <a name="kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-525">用于处理故障的展台模式行为更改</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-525">Kiosk mode behavior changes for handling of failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-526">在较旧的版本中，如果设备具有展台配置（这是全局分配的访问和 AAD 组成员分配的访问权限），则如果确定 AAD 组成员身份失败，用户将看到 "不[在启动时显示任何内容](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-kiosk#kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures)" 菜单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-526">In older builds, if a device had a kiosk configuration, which is a combination of both global assigned access and AAD group member assigned access, if determining AAD group membership failed, the user would see “[nothing shown in start](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-kiosk#kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures)” menu.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-527">从此 Windows 版本开始，kiosk 体验将回退到全局展台配置 (如果存在，则在 AAD 组展台模式发生故障的情况下) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-527">Starting in this Windows release, the kiosk experience will fallback to global kiosk configuration (if present) in case of failures during AAD group kiosk mode.</span></span>

### <a name="new-settings-uris-for-page-settings-visibility"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-528">页面设置可见性的新设置 Uri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-528">New Settings URIs for Page Settings Visibility</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-529">在 [Windows 全息版中，](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2) 我们添加了 [settings/PageVisibilityList 策略](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-settings#settings-pagevisibilitylist) ，以限制在 "设置" 应用中查看的页面20H2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-529">In [Windows Holographic, version 20H2](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2) we added the [Settings/PageVisibilityList policy](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-settings#settings-pagevisibilitylist) to restrict the pages seen within the Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-530">PageVisibilityList 是一种策略，它允许 IT 管理员阻止显示或访问 "系统设置" 应用中的特定页面，或为除指定的页面之外的所有页面执行此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-530">PageVisibilityList is a policy that allows IT Admins to either prevent specific pages in the System Settings app from being visible or accessible, or to do so for all pages except those specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-531">如果访问 [页面设置可见性](settings-uri-list.md)，则可以找到使用此 CSP 的说明，以及以前版本中可用的 uri 列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-531">If you visit [Page Settings Visibility](settings-uri-list.md), you can find instructions to use this CSP and the list of URIs available in previous releases.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-532">我们将扩展可供 IT 管理员管理的可用设置 Uri 列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-532">We are expanding upon the list of list of available Settings URIs, which IT Admins can manage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-533">其中一些 Uri 适用于新的设置应用内的新可用区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-533">Some of these URIs are for newly available areas within the new Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-534">如果你使用的是设置/PageVisibilityList 策略，请查看以下列表，并根据需要调整你允许或阻止的页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-534">If you are using Settings/PageVisibilityList policy, review the following list and adjust your allowed or blocked pages as needed.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-535">**弃用： ms 设置：网络代理**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-535">**Deprecated: ms-settings:network-proxy**</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-536">在这些较新的版本中不推荐使用一个设置页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-536">One settings page is deprecated in these newer builds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-537">旧的 **网络 & Internet**  >  **代理** 页面不再作为全局设置提供。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-537">The old **Network & Internet** > **Proxy** page is no longer available as a global setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-538">新的每连接代理设置可在 **网络 & internet**  >  **wi-fi**  >  **属性** 或 **网络 & internet**  >  **以太网**  >  **属性** 下找到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-538">The new per-connection proxy settings can be found under **Network & Internet** > **Wi-Fi** > **Properties** or **Network & Internet** > **Ethernet** > **Properties**.</span></span>

### <a name="configuring-fallback-diagnostics-via-settings-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-567">通过 "设置" 应用配置回退诊断</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-567">Configuring Fallback Diagnostics via Settings app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-568">现在，在 "设置" 应用中，用户可以配置 [回退诊断](hololens-diagnostic-logs.md)的行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-568">Now in Settings App, a user can configure the behavior of [Fallback Diagnostics](hololens-diagnostic-logs.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-569">在 "设置" 应用中，导航到 "**隐私**  ->  **故障排除**" 页以配置此设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-569">In the Settings app navigate to **Privacy** -> **Troubleshooting** page to configure this setting.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-570">如果为设备配置了 MDM 策略，则用户将无法重写该行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-570">If there is MDM policy configured for the device, user will not be able to override that behavior.</span></span>  

### <a name="share-things-with-nearby-devices"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-571">与附近设备共享东西</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-571">Share things with nearby devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-572">与 Windows 10 设备（包括电脑和其他 HoloLens 2 设备）附近共享东西。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-572">Share things with near by Windows 10 devices, including both PCs and other HoloLens 2 devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-573">可以在 "**设置**" "系统共享体验" 中试用它，  ->    ->  以将文件或 url 从 HoloLens 共享到 PC。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-573">You can try it out in **Settings** -> **System** -> **Shared Experiences** to share files or URLs from a HoloLens to a PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-574">有关更多详细信息，请参阅有关如何 [在 Windows 10 中与附近设备共享内容](https://support.microsoft.com/windows/share-things-with-nearby-devices-in-windows-10-0efbfe40-e3e2-581b-13f4-1a0e9936c2d9)的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-574">For more details read more about how to [Share things with nearby devices in Windows 10](https://support.microsoft.com/windows/share-things-with-nearby-devices-in-windows-10-0efbfe40-e3e2-581b-13f4-1a0e9936c2d9).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-575">此功能可通过 [连接/AllowConnectedDevices](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-connectivity#connectivity-allowconnecteddevices)进行管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-575">This feature can be managed via [Connectivity/AllowConnectedDevices](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-connectivity#connectivity-allowconnecteddevices).</span></span>

### <a name="new-os-diagnostic-traces"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-576">新操作系统诊断跟踪</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-576">New OS diagnostic traces</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-577">除了在 "设置" 应用程序中使用前面的疑难解答外，还添加了新的疑难解答，同时添加了新的 OS 更新设置应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-577">In addition to the previous troubleshooters within the Settings app, a new troubleshooter has been added with the addition of the new Settings app for OS Updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-578">导航到 "**设置**" "  ->  **更新 &amp; 安全**  >  **疑难解答**"  >  **Windows 更新** 并选择 "**启动**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-578">Navigate to **Settings** -> **Update &amp; Security** > **Troubleshoot** > **Windows Update** and select **Start**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-579">这样，你就可以收集跟踪，同时在操作系统更新中重现你的问题，以帮助更好地帮助你的 IT 或支持人员进行故障排除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-579">This allows you to collect traces while reproducing your issue with OS Updates to assist better in troubleshooting with your IT or support.</span></span>

### <a name="delivery-optimization-preview"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-580">传递优化预览</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-580">Delivery Optimization Preview</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-581">使用此更新，Windows 全息版可实现交付优化设置，减少从多个 HoloLens 设备下载的带宽消耗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-581">With this HoloLens update, Windows Holographic for Business enables delivery optimization settings to reduce bandwidth consumption for downloads from multiple HoloLens devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-582">此处提供了此功能以及推荐的网络配置的完整描述： [Windows 10 更新的传递优化](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/deployment/update/waas-delivery-optimization)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-582">A fuller description of this functionality along with the recommended network configuration is available here: [Delivery Optimization for Windows 10 updates](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/deployment/update/waas-delivery-optimization).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-583">以下设置作为管理界面的一部分启用， [可以从 Intune 进行配置](https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/intune/configuration/delivery-optimization-settings)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-583">The following settings are enabled as part of the management surface and [can be configured from Intune](https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/intune/configuration/delivery-optimization-settings):</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="39c90-584">DOCacheHost</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-584">DOCacheHost</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-deliveryoptimization#deliveryoptimization-docachehost)

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-596">仅限在此预览版中提供 HoloLens 支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-596">HoloLens support is limited in this preview to OS updates only.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-597">Windows 全息 for Business 仅支持 HTTP 下载模式和从 [Microsoft 连接缓存端点](https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/configmgr/core/plan-design/hierarchy/microsoft-connected-cache)下载;目前，HoloLens 设备不支持对等下载模式和组分配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-597">Windows Holographic for Business only supports HTTP download modes and downloads from a [Microsoft Connected Cache endpoint](https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/configmgr/core/plan-design/hierarchy/microsoft-connected-cache); peer-to-peer download modes and group assignments are not supported for HoloLens devices at this time.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-598">HoloLens 不支持 Windows Server Update Services 终结点的部署或传递优化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-598">HoloLens does not support deployment or delivery optimization for Windows Server Update Services endpoints.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-599">故障排除将需要在已连接的缓存服务器上进行诊断，或者通过 **设置**  >  **更新 & 安全**  >   **故障排除**  >   **Windows 更新** 在 hololens 上收集一个跟踪。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-599">Troubleshooting will require either diagnostics on the Connected Cache server or collecting a trace on HoloLens on HoloLens via **Settings** > **Update & Security** >  **Troubleshooting** >  **Windows Update**.</span></span>

### <a name="it-admin---update-checklist"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-600">IT 管理员-更新清单</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-600">IT Admin - Update Checklist</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-601">此清单可帮助你了解在此功能更新中添加的功能可能会影响当前设备管理配置的新项目，或者你可能希望开始使用的新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-601">This checklist will help you know the new items that features that are being added in this feature update that may affect your current device management configurations, or new features you might wish to start using.</span></span>

#### <a name="updates-to-kiosk-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-602">展台模式更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-602">Updates to Kiosk mode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-603">[**为展台模式下的新应用✔️新 AUMIDs**](#use-the-new-settings-and-edge-apps-in-kiosk-modes)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-603">✔️ [**New AUMIDs for new apps in Kiosk mode**](#use-the-new-settings-and-edge-apps-in-kiosk-modes):</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-604">如果你以前在展台上使用了 "设置" 应用或 "Microsoft Edge" 应用，我们已将这些应用替换为使用不同应用 ID 的新应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-604">If you were previously using either the Settings app or Microsoft Edge app in a Kiosk, we have replaced these apps with new apps which use a different App ID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-605">我们强烈建议你在下面的 [展台模式下阅读新应用的新 AUMIDs](#use-the-new-settings-and-edge-apps-in-kiosk-modes) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-605">We highly encourage you to read [New AUMIDs for new apps in Kiosk mode](#use-the-new-settings-and-edge-apps-in-kiosk-modes) below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-606">这将确保在展台中继续使用 "设置" 应用程序，或包括新的 Microsoft Edge 应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-606">This will ensure you either continue to have the Settings app in your Kiosk, or include the new Microsoft Edge app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-607">现在可以完成这些更改，并将其部署到所有设备，并允许在更新时获得更平稳的过渡效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-607">These changes can be done now, and deployed to all devices and allow for a smoother transition on update.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-608">[**网亭的✔️访问者自动登录**](#visitor-auto-logon-for-kiosks)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-608">✔️ [**Visitor Auto-logon for Kiosks**](#visitor-auto-logon-for-kiosks):</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-609">现在，访问者可以自动登录到展台。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-609">Visitors can now be automatically logged into a Kiosk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-610">默认情况下，此行为是启用的，但可以被管理和禁用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-610">This behavior is on by default but can be managed and disabled.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-611">✔️ [**改进了展台模式故障**](#kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures)处理：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-611">✔️ [**Improved Kiosk mode failure handing**](#kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures):</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-612">如果未成功确定登录 AAD 用户的 AAD 组成员身份，则会将全局展台配置用于 "开始" 菜单 (如果存在，则为 "开始" 菜单) 否则显示 "开始" 菜单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-612">If AAD group membership of signed-in AAD user is not successfully determined, then global kiosk configuration is used for start menu (if present) otherwise user is presented with empty start menu.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-613">尽管空 "开始" 菜单不是可以直接设置的配置，但如果您使用的是展台，则这种新的处理可能会告诉您的支持部门，因为这可能适用于您的配置，或者您可能想要对分配的访问配置进行新调整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-613">While the empty start menu is not a configuration you can directly set, this new handling may be something to inform your support department of if you are using Kiosks, as this may apply to your configurations or you may want to make new adjustments to your assigned access configurations.</span></span>

### <a name="improvements-and-fixes-in-the-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-628">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-628">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-631">解决了业务线应用程序安装状态报告问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-631">Fixes an issue around line of business application install status reporting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-633">修复了一个问题，该问题可能导致日语客户在边缘内键入错误的符号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-633">Fixes an issue that could lead to incorrect symbols being typed in Edge for Japanese customers.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-634">提高了 OS 更新的复原能力，如边缘的预安装应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-634">Improves the resiliency of OS updates around preinstalled apps such as Edge.</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-635">解决了影响 Microsoft Edge 安装的更新可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-635">Addresses an update reliability impacting the installation of Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

### <a name="install-apps-on-hololens-2-via-app-installer"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-683">通过应用安装程序在 HoloLens 2 上安装应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-683">Install Apps on HoloLens 2 via App Installer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-684">我们正在 **添加新功能 (应用安装程序) ，使你能够在 HoloLens 2 设备上更无缝地安装应用程序** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-684">We are **adding a new capability (App Installer) to allow you to install applications more seamlessly** on your HoloLens 2 devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-685">**默认情况下，对于非托管设备**，此功能将处于启用状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-685">The feature will be **on by default for unmanaged devices**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-686">若要防止企业中断，此时将不能 **为托管设备提供** 应用安装程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-686">To prevent disruption to enterprises, app installer will be **not be available for managed devices** at this time.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-687">如果满足以下 **任一** 条件，则将设备视为 "托管"：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-687">A device is considered “managed” if **any** of the following are true:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-688">已[注册](hololens-enroll-mdm.md)MDM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-688">MDM [Enrolled](hololens-enroll-mdm.md)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-689">配置了 [预配包](hololens-provisioning.md)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-689">Configured with [provisioning package](hololens-provisioning.md)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-690">用户 [标识](hololens-identity.md) Azure AD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-690">User [Identity](hololens-identity.md) is Azure AD</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-691">你现在可以安装应用，而无需启用开发人员模式或使用设备门户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-691">You are now able to install Apps without needing to enable Developer Mode or using Device Portal.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-692">只需通过 USB 或边缘) Appx 包下载到设备的 (，然后在文件资源管理器中导航到 Appx 捆绑，系统将提示开始安装。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-692">Simply download (over USB or through Edge) the Appx Bundle to your device and navigate to the Appx Bundle in the File Explorer to be prompted to kick off the installation.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-693">或者， [通过网页启动安装](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/msix/app-installer/installing-windows10-apps-web)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-693">Alternatively, [initiate an install from a web page](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/msix/app-installer/installing-windows10-apps-web).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-694">与使用 MDM 的 LOB 应用部署功能从 Microsoft Store 或旁加载安装的应用一样，需要使用 [签名工具](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/appxpkg/how-to-sign-a-package-using-signtool) 对应用进行数字签名，并且在部署应用之前，必须由 HoloLens 设备 [信任用于签署的证书](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/appxpkg/how-to-sign-a-package-using-signtool#security-considerations) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-694">Just like apps you install from the Microsoft Store or sideload using MDM’s LOB App deployment capability, apps need to be digitally signed with the [Sign Tool](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/appxpkg/how-to-sign-a-package-using-signtool) and the [certificate used to sign must be trusted](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/appxpkg/how-to-sign-a-package-using-signtool#security-considerations) by the HoloLens device before the app can be deployed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-695">**应用程序安装说明。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-695">**Application install instructions.**</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-696">确保你的设备不被视为托管设备</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-696">Ensure that your device is not considered managed</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-697">确保你的 HoloLens 2 设备已开机并连接到你的电脑</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-697">Ensure that your HoloLens 2 device is powered on and connected to your PC</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-698">确保已登录到 HoloLens 2 设备</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-698">Ensure that you are signed into the HoloLens 2 device</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-699">在电脑上导航到自定义应用，并将 yourapp 复制到 yourdevicename\Internal Storage\Downloads。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-699">On your PC navigate to your custom app, and copy yourapp.appxbundle to yourdevicename\Internal Storage\Downloads.</span></span>   <span data-ttu-id="39c90-700">完成文件复制后，可以断开与设备的连接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-700">After you’ve finished copying your file you can disconnect your device</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-701">从HoloLens 2打开"开始"菜单，选择"所有应用"并启动文件资源管理器应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-701">From your HoloLens 2 device Open the Start Menu, select All apps and launch the File Explorer app.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-702">导航到"下载"文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-702">Navigate to the Downloads folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-703">可能需要先在应用的左侧面板中选择"此设备"，然后导航到"下载"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-703">You may need to on the left panel of the app select This device first, then navigate to Downloads.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-704">选择 yourapp.appxbundle 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-704">Select the yourapp.appxbundle file.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-705">系统应用安装程序启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-705">The App Installer will launch.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-706">选择"安装"按钮以安装应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-706">Select the Install button to install your app.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="39c90-707">安装完成后，已安装的应用将自动启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-707">The installed app will automatically launch upon completion of installation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-708">可以在 Windows 通用示例 [GitHub](https://github.com/microsoft/Windows-universal-samples/tree/master/Samples) 上找到示例应用来测试此流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-708">You can find sample apps on [Windows Universal Samples GitHub](https://github.com/microsoft/Windows-universal-samples/tree/master/Samples) to test this flow.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-709">阅读有关使用 HoloLens 2 在 应用安装程序 [安装应用的完整过程](app-deploy-app-installer.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-709">Read about the full process of [installing apps on HoloLens 2 with the App Installer](app-deploy-app-installer.md).</span></span>

### <a name="improvements-and-fixes-in-the-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-711">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-711">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-712">手部跟踪现在在许多以前丢失手部的新情况下保持跟踪。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-712">Hand tracking now maintains tracking in many new cases where the hand previously would have been lost.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-713">在某些新情况下，只有手部位置会继续根据用户的实际手部进行更新，而其他连接则根据以前的姿势进行推断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-713">In some of these new cases, only the palm position continues to update based on the user’s real hand, while the other joints are inferred based on a previous pose.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-714">此更改有助于提高动作（如击球、引发、跳跃和击球）的跟踪一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-714">This change helps improve tracking consistency in movements such as slapping, throwing, scooping, and clapping.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-715">它还有助于手靠近表面或持有对象的情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-715">It also helps in cases where the hand is close to a surface or holding an object.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-716">在推断手部时 [，每个联合](https://docs.microsoft.com/uwp/api/windows.perception.people.jointposeaccuracy?view=winrt-19041&preserve-view=true) 准确度值将设置为"近似"，而不是"高"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-716">When hand joints are being inferred, the [per joint accuracy](https://docs.microsoft.com/uwp/api/windows.perception.people.jointposeaccuracy?view=winrt-19041&preserve-view=true) value will be set to “Approximate” instead of “High.”</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-717">修复了帐户的 PIN 重置Azure AD显示错误"出现问题的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-717">Fixed an issue where PIN reset for Azure AD accounts would show an error "Something went wrong.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-718">启动 ET、设置应用中的 Iris、新用户或通知 toast 时，用户应看到更少的启动后 OOBE 故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-718">Users should see much less post-boot OOBE crashes when launching ET, Iris from settings app, new user, or notification toast.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-719">用户应具有来自 OOBE 的正确时区。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-719">Users should have correct time zone coming out of OOBE.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-722">此每月质量更新不包含任何值得注意的更改，建议试用最新的 Windows Holographic 版本 20H2 – 2020 年 12 月更新和内部版本中新增的 应用安装程序 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-722">This monthly quality update doesn't contain any notable changes, we encourage you to try out our latest Windows Holographic, version 20H2 – December 2020 Update and the new App Installer feature added in the build.</span></span>


## <a name="windows-holographic-version-20h2"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-723">Windows Holographic 版本 20H2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-723">Windows Holographic, version 20H2</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-724">内部版本 19041.1128</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-724">Build 19041.1128</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-725">Windows Holographic 版本 20H2 现已发布，为用户和 IT 专业人员HoloLens 2一系列新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-725">Windows Holographic, version 20H2 is now available and brings a great set of new features to HoloLens 2 users and IT professionals.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-726">从"自动眼定位"到"设置"中的证书管理器，到改进的展台模式功能和新的 Autopilot 设置功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-726">From Auto Eye Positioning, to Certificate Manager in Settings, to improved Kiosk Mode functionality, and new Autopilot setup capabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-727">此新更新使 IT 团队能够更精细地控制 HoloLens 设备的配置和管理，并为用户提供更无缝的全息体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-727">This new update enables IT teams to take more granular control to configuring and managing HoloLens devices, and offers users even more seamless holographic experiences.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-728">此最新版本是版本 2004 的每月更新，但这次我们将包含新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-728">This latest release is a monthly update to version 2004, but this time we are including new features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-729">主内部版本号将保持不变，Windows 更新版本 2004 (版本 19041 版本) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-729">The major build number will remain the same and Windows Update will indicate a monthly release to version 2004 (build 19041).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-730">可以在"设置"的"关于>中查看"生成号"，以确认你位于最新的可用内部版本 19041.1128+ 上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-730">You can look at your Build Number in your Settings > About screen to confirm you are on the latest available build 19041.1128+.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-731">若要更新到最新版本，请打开"设置"应用，转到"更新&安全性"，然后点击"检查更新"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-731">To update to the latest release, open the Settings app, go to Update & Security, and tap Check for Updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-732">若要详细了解如何管理 HoloLens 更新，请访问 [此页](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-updates)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-732">For more information on how to manage HoloLens updates, visit [this page](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-updates).</span></span>

### <a name="auto-eye-position-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-774">自动眼部位置支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-774">Auto Eye Position Support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-775">在HoloLens 2中，眼部位置可实现准确的全息影像定位、舒适观看体验和改进的显示质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-775">In HoloLens 2, eye positions enable accurate hologram positioning, comfortable viewing experience and improved display quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-776">眼部位置作为眼动跟踪计算的一部分在内部计算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-776">Eye positions are computed internally as part of the eye tracking computation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-777">但是，这要求每个用户进行眼动跟踪校准，即使体验可能不需要眼睛凝视输入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-777">However, this requires each user to go through eye tracking calibration, even when the experience might not require eye gaze input.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-778">**自动眼 (AEP)** 通过无交互方式为用户计算眼睛位置，从而启用这些方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-778">**Auto Eye Position (AEP)** enables these scenarios with an interaction-free way to compute eye positions for the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-779">自动眼睛位置从用户打开设备那一刻开始自动在后台工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-779">Auto Eye Position starts working in the background automatically from the moment the user puts the device on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-780">如果用户没有以前的眼动跟踪校准，则自动眼部定位将在处理 20 - 30 秒后开始向显示系统提供用户眼睛位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-780">If the user does not have a prior eye tracking calibration, Auto Eye Position will start providing the user's eye positions to the display system after a processing time of 20 - 30 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-781">用户数据不会持久保存在设备上，因此，如果用户关闭并重新启动设备，或者设备重新启动或从睡眠状态唤醒，则重复此过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-781">The user data is not persisted on the device and hence this process is repeated if the user takes off and puts the device back on or if the device reboots or wakes up from sleep.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-782">当未校准的用户置于设备上时，自动眼睛位置功能存在一些系统行为更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-782">There are a few system behavior changes with Auto Eye Position feature when an uncalibrated user puts on the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-783">在此上下文中，未校准的用户是指以前未在设备上完成眼动跟踪校准过程的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-783">In this context, an uncalibrated user refers to someone who has not gone through the eye tracking calibration process on the device previously.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="39c90-784">活动应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-784">Active Application</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="39c90-785">以前的行为</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-785">Prior Behavior</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="39c90-786">Windows Holographic 版本 20H2 更新中的行为</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-786">Behavior from Windows Holographic, version 20H2 Update</span></span> |
|:-------------------|:-----------------|:-----------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="39c90-787">未启用凝视的应用或 Holographic Shell</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-787">Non-gaze enabled app or Holographic Shell</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="39c90-788">显示眼动跟踪校准提示对话框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-788">Eye tracking calibration prompt dialog is displayed.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="39c90-789">不显示提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-789">No prompt is displayed.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="39c90-790">已启用凝视的应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-790">Gaze enabled app</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="39c90-791">显示眼动跟踪校准提示对话框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-791">Eye tracking calibration prompt dialog is displayed.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="39c90-792">只有在应用程序访问眼睛凝视流时，才显示眼动跟踪校准提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-792">Eye tracking calibration prompt is displayed only when the application accesses eye gaze stream.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-793">如果用户从未启用凝视的应用程序转换为访问凝视数据的应用程序，将显示校准提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-793">If the user transitions from a non-gaze enabled application to one that accesses the gaze data, the calibration prompt will be displayed.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-794">当当前用户没有活动的眼动跟踪校准时，所有其他系统行为将类似于 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-794">All other system behavior will be similar to when the current user does not have an active eye tracking calibration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-795">例如，不会启用单手启动手势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-795">For example, the One-handed Start gesture will not be enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-796">初始设置时，不会更改"开箱即用体验"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-796">There will be no change to the Out-Of-Box-Experience for initial setup.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-797">对于需要眼睛凝视数据或非常精确的全息影像定位的体验，我们建议未校准的用户运行眼动跟踪校准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-797">For experiences that require eye gaze data or very precise hologram positioning, we recommend uncalibrated users to run eye tracking calibration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-798">可以通过眼动跟踪校准提示或从开始菜单启动"设置"应用，然后选择"系统"">校准 **">""** 眼>校准"来访问它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-798">It is accessible from the eye tracking calibration prompt or by launching the Settings app from the start menu, and then selecting **System > Calibration > Eye Calibration > Run eye calibration**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-799">稍后可与其他校准信息 [一起找到此信息](hololens-calibration.md#auto-eye-position-support)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-799">This information can be found later with [other calibration information](hololens-calibration.md#auto-eye-position-support).</span></span> 

### <a name="certificate-manager"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-800">证书管理器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-800">Certificate Manager</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-801">通过新的证书管理器改进了设备安全性和符合性的审核、诊断和验证工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-801">Improved auditing, diagnosis, and validation tooling for device security and compliance through the new Certificate Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-802">此功能可让你在商业环境中大规模部署、排查和验证证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-802">This capability will enable you to deploy, troubleshoot, and validate your certificates at scale in commercial environments.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-803">在 Windows Holographic 版本 20H2 中，我们将在"设置"应用中添加HoloLens 2管理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-803">In Windows Holographic version 20H2, we are adding a Certificate Manager in the HoloLens 2 Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-804">转到"**设置>更新&安全>证书"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-804">Go to **Settings > Update & Security > Certificates**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-805">此功能提供了一种简单且用户友好的方式来查看、安装和删除设备上证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-805">This feature provides a simple and user-friendly way to view, install and remove certificates on your device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-806">借助新的证书管理器，管理员和用户现在改进了审核、诊断和验证工具，以确保设备保持安全且合规。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-806">With the new Certificate Manager, admins and users now have improved auditing, diagnosis and validation tooling to ensure that devices remain secure and compliant.</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="39c90-807">**审核：** 能够验证证书是否正确部署，或确认证书已正确删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-807">**Auditing:** Ability to validate that a certificate is deployed correctly or to confirm that it was removed appropriately.</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="39c90-808">**诊断：** 出现问题时，验证设备上是否存在相应的证书可节省时间，并有助于进行故障排除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-808">**Diagnosis:** When issues arise, validating that the appropriate certificates exist on the device saves time and helps with troubleshooting.</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="39c90-809">**验证：** 验证证书是否符合预期目的且正常运行，可以节省大量时间，尤其是在商业环境中，然后再大规模部署证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-809">**Validation:** Verifying that a certificate serves the intended purpose and is functional, can save significant time, particularly in commercial environments before deploying certificates at larger scale.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-810">若要在列表中快速查找特定证书，有一些选项可以按名称、存储或到期日期进行排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-810">To find a specific certificate in the list quickly, there are options to sort by name, store or expiration date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-811">用户还可以直接搜索证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-811">Users may also directly search for a certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-812">若要查看单个证书属性，请选择证书，然后单击"信息 **"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-812">To view individual certificate properties, select the certificate and click on **Info**.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-813">证书安装当前支持 .cer 和 .crt 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-813">Certificate installation currently supports .cer and .crt files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-814">设备所有者可以在本地计算机和当前用户中安装证书; 所有其他用户只能安装到当前用户中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-814">Device Owners can install certificates in Local Machine and Current User;  all other users can only install into Current User.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-815">用户只能从"设置"UI 中删除直接安装的证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-815">Users can only remove certificates installed directly from the Settings UI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-816">如果证书是通过其他方式安装的，则还必须使用相同的机制将其删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-816">If a certificate has been installed through other means, it must also be removed by the same mechanism.</span></span>

#### <a name="to-install-a-certificate"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-817">安装证书：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-817">To install a certificate:</span></span> 

1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-818">将HoloLens 2连接到电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-818">Connect your HoloLens 2 to a PC.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-819">将要安装的证书文件放在证书HoloLens 2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-819">Place the certificate file you want to install in a location on your HoloLens 2.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-820">导航到" **设置>更新&安全>证书"，** 然后选择"安装证书"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-820">Navigate to **Settings App > Update & Security > Certificates**, and select Install a certificate.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-821">单击 **"导入** 文件"并导航到保存证书的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-821">Click **Import File** and navigate to the location you saved the certificate.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-822">选择"**存储位置"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-822">Select **Store Location**.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-823">选择 **"证书存储"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-823">Select **Certificate Store**.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="39c90-824">单击“安装”  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-824">Click **Install**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-825">现在应在设备上安装证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-825">The certificate should now be installed on the device.</span></span>

#### <a name="to-remove-a-certificate"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-826">删除证书：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-826">To remove a certificate:</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-827">导航到"**设置应用>更新和安全>证书"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-827">Navigate to **Settings App > Update and Security > Certificates**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-828">在搜索框中按名称搜索证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-828">Search for the certificate by name in the search box.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-829">选择证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-829">Select the certificate.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-830">单击" **删除"**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-830">Click **Remove**</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-831">出现确认提示时，选择“是”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-831">Select **Yes** when prompted for confirmation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-834">稍后可在新的"证书管理器 ["页上找到此信息](certificate-manager.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-834">This information can be found later [on a new Certificate Manager page](certificate-manager.md).</span></span>

### <a name="auto-launch-provisioning-from-usb"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-835">从 USB 自动启动预配</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-835">Auto-launch provisioning from USB</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-836">在 OOBE 期间使用带预配包的 USB 驱动器时，自动化过程允许较少的用户交互。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-836">Automated processes allowing for less user interaction, when USB Drives with Provisioning Packages are used during OOBE.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-837">在此版本之前，用户必须手动在 OOBE 期间启动预配屏幕，才能使用按钮组合进行预配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-837">Before this release users had to launch the provisioning screen manually during OOBE to provision using a button combination.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-838">现在，用户可以通过使用 USB 存储驱动器上的预配包跳过按钮组合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-838">Now users can skip the button combination, by using a Provisioning Package on a USB storage drive.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-839">在 OOBE 的第一个可交互时刻使用预配包插入 USB 驱动器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-839">Plug in the USB drive with the provisioning package during OOBE’s first interactable moment</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-840">当设备准备好进行预配时，它会自动打开包含预配页的提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-840">When the device is ready to be provisioned it will automatically open the prompt with the provisioning page.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-841">注意：如果在设备启动时 USB 驱动器已接通电源，则 OOBE 将枚举现有的 USB 存储设备，并监视插入的其他 USB 存储设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-841">Note: If a USB drive is left plugged in while the device is booting then OOBE will enumerate existing USB storage device, as well as watch for additional ones being plugged in.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-842">有关在 OOBE 期间应用预配包的信息，请访问 [HoloLens 预配](hololens-provisioning.md#apply-a-provisioning-package-to-hololens-during-setup) 文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-842">For more information about applying provisioning packages during OOBE, visit the [HoloLens provisioning](hololens-provisioning.md#apply-a-provisioning-package-to-hololens-during-setup) documentation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-843">有关从 [USB 自动启动预配](hololens-provisioning.md#auto-launch-provisioning-from-usb) 的其他信息，请参阅 HoloLens 预配文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-843">Additional information on [auto-launch provisioning from a USB](hololens-provisioning.md#auto-launch-provisioning-from-usb) can be found in the HoloLens provisioning documentation.</span></span>

### <a name="auto-confirm-provisioning-packages-in-oobe"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-844">在 OOBE 中自动确认预配包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-844">Auto-confirm provisioning packages in OOBE</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-845">自动化过程允许较少的用户交互，当显示"预配包"页时，它将自动应用列出的所有包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-845">Automated process allowing for less user interaction, when the Provisioning Package page is displayed it will automatically apply all packages listed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-846">当预配主屏幕出现时，OOBE 将倒计时 10 秒，然后自动开始应用所有预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-846">When the provisioning main screen comes up, OOBE will count down 10 seconds before automatically starting applying all provisioning packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-847">在验证 [预期的包](hololens-provisioning.md#auto-confirm-provisioning-packages-in-oobe) 后，用户仍然可以在此 10 秒内确认或取消。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-847">Users can still [confirm or cancel](hololens-provisioning.md#auto-confirm-provisioning-packages-in-oobe) within this 10 seconds after verifying the packages they expected.</span></span>

### <a name="automatic-provisioning-without-using-ui"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-848">无需使用 UI 即可自动预配</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-848">Automatic provisioning without using UI</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-849">合并了自动过程，减少了预配的设备交互。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-849">Combined automatic processes for reduced device interactions for provisioning.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-850">通过将从 USB 设备自动启动预配和自动确认预配包相结合，用户可以自动预配 HoloLens 2 设备，而无需使用设备的 UI，甚至无需设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-850">By combining the auto-launch of provisioning from USB devices and the auto-confirmation of provisioning packages, a user can provision HoloLens 2 devices automatically without using the device's UI or even wearing the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-851">你可以继续为多个设备使用相同的 USB 驱动器和预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-851">You may continue to use the same USB drive and provisioning package for multiple devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-852">这可用于在同一区域中一次部署多个设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-852">This is useful for deploying multiple devices at once in the same area.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-853">[使用 Windows 配置设计器 创建](hololens-provisioning.md)[预配包](https://www.microsoft.com/store/productId/9NBLGGH4TX22)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-853">[Create a Provisioning Package](hololens-provisioning.md) using [Windows Configuration Designer](https://www.microsoft.com/store/productId/9NBLGGH4TX22).</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-854">将包复制到 USB 存储驱动器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-854">Copy the package to a USB storage drive.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-855">[将HoloLens 2](hololens-insider.md#ffu-download-and-flash-directions)刷新到[19041.1361 或更高版本。](https://aka.ms/hololens2previewdownload)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-855">[Flash your HoloLens 2](hololens-insider.md#ffu-download-and-flash-directions) to [19041.1361 or newer build](https://aka.ms/hololens2previewdownload).</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-856">高级 [恢复助手](https://www.microsoft.com/store/productId/9P74Z35SFRS8) 完成刷用设备后，拔下 USB-C 电缆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-856">When [Advanced Recovery Companion](https://www.microsoft.com/store/productId/9P74Z35SFRS8) has completed flashing your device unplug your USB-C cable.</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-857">将 USB 驱动器插入设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-857">Plug in your USB drive to the device.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-858">当HoloLens 2设备启动到 OOBE 时，它会自动检测 USB 驱动器上的预配包并启动预配页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-858">When the HoloLens 2 device boots into OOBE it will automatically detect the provisioning package on the USB drive and launch the provisioning page.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-859">10 秒后，设备将自动应用预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-859">After 10 seconds the device will automatically apply the provisioning package.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-860">设备现已配置，将显示 ["预配成功"屏幕](hololens-provisioning.md#automatic-provisioning-without-using-ui)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-860">Your device is now configured and will [display the Provisioning Successful screen](hololens-provisioning.md#automatic-provisioning-without-using-ui).</span></span>

### <a name="using-autopilot-with-wi-fi-connection"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-861">将 Autopilot 与 Wi-Fi连接一起使用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-861">Using Autopilot with Wi-Fi connection</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-862">通过使 Autopilot 在连接的设备上运行，无需使用 USB-C 适配器Wi-Fi硬件需求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-862">Removed need for USB-C adapters to ethernet reducing hardware needs, by enabling Autopilot to function on Wi-Fi connected devices.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-863">现在，在 OOBE 期间，HoloLens 2连接到 Wi-Fi 后，OOBE 将检查设备的 Autopilot 配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-863">Now during OOBE, once you connect HoloLens 2 with Wi-Fi, OOBE will check for an Autopilot profile for the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-864">如果找到一个，它将用于完成 AAD 联接和注册流的其余部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-864">If one is found it will be used to complete rest of the AAD join and enrollment flow.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-865">换句话说，不再要求使用以太网到 USB-C 或Wi-Fi连接到 USB-C 适配器，但如果在 OOBE 开始时提供，它们将继续工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-865">In other words, using ethernet to USB-C or Wi-Fi to USB-C adapter is not a requirement anymore, however they continue to work if provided at beginning of OOBE.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-866">详细了解适用于[设备 HoloLens 2 Autopilot。](hololens2-autopilot.md)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-866">Learn more about [Autopilot for HoloLens 2 devices](hololens2-autopilot.md).</span></span>

### <a name="tenantlockdown-csp-and-autopilot"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-867">Tenantlockdown CSP 和 Autopilot</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-867">Tenantlockdown CSP and Autopilot</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-868">通过锁定组织租户上的设备，即使设备重置或重启，也可以将设备锁定到租户中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-868">Keeps devices on the organization's tenant by locking them to the tenant even through device reset or reflash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-869">通过禁止通过预配在 中创建帐户，进一步实现安全性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-869">With further security by disallowing account creation in via provisioning.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-870">HoloLens 2 Windows Holographic 版本 [20H2](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2)起，所有设备现在都支持 TenantLockdown CSP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-870">HoloLens 2 devices now support TenantLockdown CSP as of [Windows Holographic version 20H2](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2).</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-871">[TenantLockdown](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/tenantlockdown-csp) CSP 使HoloLens 2仅与使用 Autopilot 的 MDM 注册绑定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-871">[TenantLockdown](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/tenantlockdown-csp) CSP enables HoloLens 2 to be tied to MDM enrollment using Autopilot only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-872">将 TenantLockdown CSP 的 RequireNetworkInOOBE 节点设置为 true 或 false (最初在 HoloLens 2 上设置) 值后，该值将保留在设备上，而不管重新闪烁、OS 更新等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-872">Once TenantLockdown CSP’s RequireNetworkInOOBE node is set to either true or false (initially set) value on HoloLens 2, that value remains on the device despite re-flashing, OS updates, etc.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-873">在 HoloLens 2 上将 TenantLockdown CSP 的 RequireNetworkInOOBE 节点设置为 true 后，OOBE 将无限期等待 Autopilot 配置文件在网络连接后成功下载并应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-873">Once TenantLockdown CSPs’ RequireNetworkInOOBE node is set to true on HoloLens 2, OOBE waits indefinitely for Autopilot profile to be successfully downloaded and applied, after network connectivity.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-874">当 TenantLockdown CSP 的 RequireNetworkInOOBE 节点在 HoloLens 2 设置为 true 后，OOBE 中将禁止以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-874">Once TenantLockdown CSPs’ RequireNetworkInOOBE node is set to true on HoloLens 2, following operations are disallowed in OOBE:</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-875">使用运行时预配创建本地用户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-875">Creating local user using runtime provisioning</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-876">通过Azure AD执行联接操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-876">Performing Azure AD join operation via runtime provisioning</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-877">选择在 OOBE 体验中拥有设备的人</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-877">Selecting who owns the device in OOBE experience</span></span> 

#### <a name="how-to-set-this-using-intune"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-878">如何使用 Intune 设置此设置？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-878">How to set this using Intune?</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-879">创建自定义 OMA URI 设备配置文件，并指定 RequireNetworkInOOBE 节点的 true，如下所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-879">Create a custom OMA URI device configuration profile and specify true for RequireNetworkInOOBE node as shown below.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="39c90-880">OMA-URI 值应为 ./Vendor/MSFT/TenantLockdown/RequireNetworkInOOBE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-880">OMA-URI value should be ./Vendor/MSFT/TenantLockdown/RequireNetworkInOOBE</span></span>

   > [!div class="mx-imgBorder"]
   > <span data-ttu-id="39c90-881">![通过 OMA-URI 设置锁定](images/hololens-tenant-lockdown.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-881">![Setting tennant lockdown via OMA-URI](images/hololens-tenant-lockdown.png)</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-882">创建一个组，并将设备配置文件分配给该设备组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-882">Create a group and assign the device configuration profile to that device group.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-883">使HoloLens 2在上一步中创建的组的设备成员，并触发同步。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-883">Make the HoloLens 2 device member of the group created in previous step and trigger sync.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-884">在 Intune 门户中验证设备配置是否已成功应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-884">Verify in the Intune portal that device configuration has been successfully applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-885">此设备配置成功应用于 HoloLens 2后，TenantLockdown 的效果将处于活动状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-885">Once this device configuration successfully applies on the HoloLens 2 device, effects of TenantLockdown will be active.</span></span>

#### <a name="how-to-unset-tenantlockdowns-requirenetworkinoobe-on-hololens-2-using-intune"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-886">如何使用 Intune 在 HoloLens 2上取消设置 TenantLockdown 的 RequireNetworkInOOBE？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-886">How to unset TenantLockdown’s RequireNetworkInOOBE on HoloLens 2 using Intune?</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-887">从HoloLens 2之前为其分配了设备配置的设备组中删除该配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-887">Remove the HoloLens 2 from the device group to which the device configuration created above was previously assigned.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-888">创建自定义基于 OMA URI 的设备配置文件，并指定 RequireNetworkInOOBE 的 false，如下所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-888">Create a custom OMA URI based device configuration profile and specify false for RequireNetworkInOOBE as shown below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-889">OMA-URI 值应为 ./Vendor/MSFT/TenantLockdown/RequireNetworkInOOBE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-889">OMA-URI value should be ./Vendor/MSFT/TenantLockdown/RequireNetworkInOOBE</span></span>

   > [!div class="mx-imgBorder"]
   > <span data-ttu-id="39c90-890">![通过 Intune 中的 OMA URI 将 RequireNetworkInOOBE 设置为 false 的屏幕截图](images/hololens-tenant-lockdown-false.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-890">![Screenshot of setting RequireNetworkInOOBE to false via OMA URI in Intune](images/hololens-tenant-lockdown-false.png)</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-891">创建一个组，并将设备配置文件分配给该设备组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-891">Create a group and assign the device configuration profile to that device group.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-892">使HoloLens 2在上一步中创建的组的设备成员，并触发同步。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-892">Make the HoloLens 2 device member of the group created in previous step and trigger sync.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-893">在 Intune 门户中验证设备配置是否已成功应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-893">Verify in the Intune portal that device configuration has been successfully applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-894">此设备配置成功应用于 HoloLens 2后，TenantLockdown 的影响将处于非活动状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-894">Once this device configuration successfully applies on the HoloLens 2 device, effects of TenantLockdown will be inactive.</span></span> 

#### <a name="what-would-happen-during-oobe-if-autopilot-profile-is-unassigned-on-a-hololens-after-tenantlockdown-was-set-to-true"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-895">如果在 TenantLockdown 设置为 true 后在 HoloLens 上取消分配 Autopilot 配置文件，在 OOBE 期间会发生什么情况？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-895">What would happen during OOBE, if Autopilot profile is unassigned on a HoloLens after TenantLockdown was set to true?</span></span> 
<span data-ttu-id="39c90-896">OOBE 将无限期等待 Autopilot 配置文件下载，并会显示以下对话框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-896">OOBE will wait indefinitely for Autopilot profile to download and following dialog will be presented.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-897">若要消除 TenantLockdown 的影响，设备必须先使用 Autopilot 注册到其原始租户，并且 RequireNetworkInOOBE 必须取消设置，如上一步所述，然后才能删除 TenantLockdown CSP 引入的限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-897">In order to remove effects of TenantLockdown, device must be enrolled with its original tenant first using Autopilot only and RequireNetworkInOOBE must be unset as described in previous step before restrictions introduced by TenantLockdown CSP are removed.</span></span> 

![设备内视图，显示何时在设备上强制实施策略。](images/hololens-autopilot-lockdown.png)

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-899">现在，可以在 [Tenantlockdown CSP 和 Autopilot](hololens2-autopilot.md#tenantlockdown-csp-and-autopilot)下与 Autopilot 的其余部分一起找到此信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-899">This information can now be found alongside the rest of Autopilot under [Tenantlockdown CSP and Autopilot](hololens2-autopilot.md#tenantlockdown-csp-and-autopilot).</span></span>

### <a name="global-assigned-access--kiosk-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-900">全局分配访问权限 - 展台模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-900">Global Assigned Access – Kiosk Mode</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-901">通过启用在系统级别应用展台模式的新展台方法，减少了展台的标识管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-901">Reduced Identity management for Kiosk, by enabling new Kiosk method that applies Kiosk mode at the system level.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-902">此新功能允许 IT 管理员为多个应用展台模式配置 HoloLens 2 设备，该模式适用于系统级别，与系统上的任何标识没有关联，并且适用于登录设备的每个人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-902">This new feature allows an IT Admin to configure a HoloLens 2 device for multiple app kiosk mode which is applicable at system level, has no affinity with any identity on the system and applies to everyone who signs into the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-903">在 [HoloLens](hololens-global-assigned-access-kiosk.md)全局分配访问展台 中详细了解此新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-903">Read about this new feature in detail in the [HoloLens global assigned access kiosk](hololens-global-assigned-access-kiosk.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-906">仅适用于多应用展台模式，并且只能使用"分配的访问权限配置"中下面的突出显示属性将 1 个应用指定为自动启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-906">Applies only to multiple-app kiosk mode and only 1 app can be designated to auto-launch using highlighted attribute below in Assigned Access configuration.</span></span>

### <a name="kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-908">展台模式行为更改，用于处理故障</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-908">Kiosk mode behavior changes for handling of failures</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-909">通过消除展台模式故障时可用的应用，实现更安全的展台模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-909">More secure Kiosk mode by eliminating available apps on Kiosk mode failures.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-910">在应用展台模式时遇到故障之前，HoloLens 用于在开始菜单中显示所有应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-910">Earlier on encountering failures in applying kiosk mode, HoloLens used to show up all applications in start menu.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-911">现在，在 Windows Holographic 版本 20H2 中，如果出现故障，开始菜单中不会显示任何应用，如下所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-911">Now in Windows Holographic version 20H2 in the case of failures no apps will be shown in the start menu as below:</span></span>

### <a name="cache-azure-ad-group-membership-for-offline-kiosk"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-937">缓存Azure AD展台的组成员身份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-937">Cache Azure AD Group membership for offline Kiosk</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-938">已启用脱机展台，可与 AAD 组一起使用最多 60 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-938">Enabled Offline Kiosks to be used with AAD groups for up to 60 days.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-939">此策略控制多少天，Azure AD组成员身份缓存用于针对已登录用户Azure AD组分配的访问配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-939">This policy controls for how many days, Azure AD group membership cache is allowed to be used for Assigned Access configurations targeting Azure AD groups for signed in user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-940">一旦此策略值设置为大于 0 的值，则否则使用缓存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-940">Once this policy value is set to value greater than 0 only then cache is used otherwise not.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-941">名称：AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays URI 值：./Vendor/MSFT/Policy/Config/MixedReality/AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-941">Name: AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays URI value: ./Vendor/MSFT/Policy/Config/MixedReality/AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-942">最短 - 0 天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-942">Min - 0 days</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="39c90-943">最大值 - 60 天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-943">Max - 60 days</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-944">正确使用此策略的步骤：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-944">Steps to use this policy correctly:</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-945">为展台组创建设备配置文件，Azure AD并将其分配给 HoloLens (设备) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-945">Create a device configuration profile for kiosk targeting Azure AD groups and assign it to HoloLens device(s).</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-946">创建基于 OMA URI 的自定义设备配置，将此策略值设置为所需的天数 (> 0) 并将其分配给 HoloLens () 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-946">Create a custom OMA URI based device configuration which sets this policy value to desired number of days (> 0) and assign it to HoloLens device(s).</span></span> 
    1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-947">URI 值应在 OMA-URI 文本框中输入为 ./Vendor/MSFT/Policy/Config/MixedReality/AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-947">The URI value should be entered in OMA-URI text box as ./Vendor/MSFT/Policy/Config/MixedReality/AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-948">该值可以介于允许的最小值/最大值之间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-948">The value can be between min / max allowed.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-949">注册 HoloLens 设备，并验证这两种配置是否应用到设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-949">Enroll HoloLens devices and verify both configurations get applied to the device.</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-950">在Azure AD Internet 可用时让用户 1 登录，用户登录并成功Azure AD组成员身份后，将创建缓存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-950">Let Azure AD user 1 sign-in when internet is available, once user signs-in and Azure AD group membership is confirmed successfully, cache will be created.</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-951">现在Azure AD用户 1 可以脱机使用 HoloLens，只要策略值允许 X 天，就可以将 HoloLens 用于展台模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-951">Now Azure AD user 1 can take HoloLens offline and use it for kiosk mode as long as policy value allows for X number of days.</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-952">对于任何其他 Azure AD 用户 N，可以重复步骤 4 和 5。此处的要点是，任何 Azure AD 用户都必须使用 Internet 登录到设备，以便我们至少能够确定他们是展台配置所面向的 Azure AD 组的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-952">Steps 4 and 5 can be repeated for any other Azure AD user N. Key point here is that any Azure AD user must sign-in to device using Internet so at least once we can determine that they are member of Azure AD group to which Kiosk configuration is targeted.</span></span> 
 
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-953">在针对用户执行步骤 4 之前Azure AD用户将遇到"断开连接"环境中提到的失败行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-953">Until step 4 is performed for a Azure AD user will experience failure behavior mentioned in “disconnected” environments.</span></span> 

### <a name="new-device-restriction-policies-for-hololens-2"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-954">新的设备限制策略HoloLens 2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-954">New device restriction policies for HoloLens 2</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-955">允许用户管理特定的设备管理策略，例如阻止添加或删除预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-955">Allows users to manage specific device management policies such as blocking adding or removing provisioning packages.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-956">新启用的策略，允许对设备HoloLens 2选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-956">Newly enabled policies that allow for more management options of HoloLens 2 devices.</span></span> 
- [<span data-ttu-id="39c90-957">AllowAddProvisioningPackage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-957">AllowAddProvisioningPackage</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-security#security-allowaddprovisioningpackage)
- [<span data-ttu-id="39c90-958">AllowRemoveProvisioningPackage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-958">AllowRemoveProvisioningPackage</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-security#security-allowremoveprovisioningpackage) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="39c90-959">ConfigureTimeZone</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-959">ConfigureTimeZone</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-timelanguagesettings#timelanguagesettings-configuretimezone)
- [<span data-ttu-id="39c90-960">RemoteLock</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-960">RemoteLock</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/remotelock-csp)

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-962">对于 RemoteLock，HoloLens 将仅支持 ./Vendor/MSFT/RemoteLock/Lock 配置。 [](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/remotelock-csp)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-962">In regard to [RemoteLock](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/remotelock-csp), HoloLens will only support the ./Vendor/MSFT/RemoteLock/Lock configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-963">不支持处理 PIN 的配置，例如重置和恢复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-963">The configurations dealing with PIN such as reset and recover are not supported.</span></span>
