### <a name="research-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1001">研究模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1001">Research mode</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1002">在研究模式下，HoloLens 2成为计算机视觉研究的重要工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1002">While in Research Mode, the HoloLens 2 becomes a potent tool for computer vision research.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1003">与以前的版本相比，HoloLens 2研究模式具有以下优点：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1003">Compared to previous editions, Research Mode for HoloLens 2 has the following advantages:</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1004">除了在 HoloLens (第一代) 研究模式下公开的传感器外，我们现在提供 IMU 传感器访问，包括加速计、陀螺仪和磁力计。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1004">In addition to sensors exposed in HoloLens (1st gen) Research Mode, we now provide IMU sensor access including an accelerometer, gyroscope, and magnetometer.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1005">HoloLens 2提供了可以与研究模式一起使用的新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1005">HoloLens 2 provides new capabilities that can be used together with Research Mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1006">具体而言，可以访问可交付更丰富试验集的表达式手部跟踪和眼动跟踪 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1006">Specifically, access to articulated hand-tracking and eye-tracking APIs that can deliver a richer set of experiments.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1007">研究人员现在可以选择在 HoloLens 设备上启用研究模式，以访问所有这些面向外部的原始图像传感器流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1007">Researchers now have the option of enabling Research Mode on their HoloLens devices to access all of these external facing raw image sensors streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1008">研究模式HoloLens 2提供对加速计、陀螺仪和磁力计读数的访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1008">Research Mode for HoloLens 2 also provides access to the accelerometer, gyroscope, and magnetometer readings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1009">为了保护用户的隐私，无法通过研究模式使用原始眼动跟踪相机图像，但可以通过现有 API 获得眼睛凝视方向。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1009">To protect users’ privacy, raw eye-tracking camera images are not available through Research Mode, but eye-gaze direction  is available through existing APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1010">有关更多 [技术详细信息，请查看](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/research-mode) 研究模式文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1010">Check out the [Research Mode documentation](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/research-mode) for further technical details.</span></span>

### <a name="recording-length-increased"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1011">录制长度增加</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1011">Recording length increased</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1012">根据客户反馈，我们增加了混合现实捕获 [的录制长度](holographic-photos-and-videos.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1012">Due to customer feedback we’ve increased the recording length of [mixed reality captures](holographic-photos-and-videos.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1013">默认情况下，混合现实捕获将不再限制为 5 分钟，而是根据可用磁盘空间计算最大录制长度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1013">Mixed reality captures will no longer be limited to 5 minutes by default but instead will calculate the maximum recording length based on available disk space.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1014">设备将基于可用磁盘空间估计最大视频录制持续时间，最多占总磁盘空间的 80%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1014">The device will estimate the max video recording duration based on available disk space up to 80% of the total disk space.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1015">如果发生下列情况之一 (HoloLens) 5 分钟：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1015">The HoloLens will use default video recording length (5 minutes) if one of the following occurs:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1016">估计的最大录制持续时间小于默认的 5 分钟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1016">The estimated max recording duration is smaller than the default 5 mins.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1017">可用磁盘空间小于总磁盘空间的 20%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1017">The available disk space is less than 20% of the total disk space.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1018">可以在全息照片和视频文档中 [找到完整](holographic-photos-and-videos.md#maximum-recording-length) 要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1018">You can find the full requirements in our [holographic photos and videos](holographic-photos-and-videos.md#maximum-recording-length) documentation.</span></span> 

### <a name="improvements-and-fixes-in-the-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1019">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1019">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1020">OOBE 中的更多屏幕现在以深色模式显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1020">More screens in OOBE  are now in dark mode.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1021">了解更多内容应指向最新的联机隐私声明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1021">Learn more content should point to the latest Privacy Statement online.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1022">解决了用户无法通过预配包预配 VPN 配置文件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1022">Addressed an issue where users could not provision VPN profiles through provisioning packages.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1023">修复了 VPN 连接的代理配置问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1023">Fixed proxy configuration issue for VPN connection.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1024">更新了策略，以禁用通过适用于 NCM for AllowUsbConnection 的 MDM 枚举 USB 函数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1024">Updated policy to disable enumeration of USB functions through MDM for NCM for AllowUsbConnection.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1025">解决了在将 HoloLens 设备设置为单应用展台时，无法通过媒体传输协议 (MTP) 在 文件资源管理器 中显示 HoloLens 设备 [的问题](hololens-kiosk.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1025">Addressed an issue that prevented a HoloLens device from showing up in File Explorer over Media Transfer Protocol (MTP) when the device is set up as a [single-app kiosk](hololens-kiosk.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1026">请注意，通常 (使用 [AllowUSBConnection](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-connectivity#connectivity-allowusbconnection) 策略) 禁用 MTP 连接和 USB 连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1026">Note that MTP (and USB connection in general) can still be disabled using the [AllowUSBConnection](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-connectivity#connectivity-allowusbconnection) policy.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1027">修复了在展台模式下正确缩放“开始”菜单图标的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1027">Fixed an issue where icons in the Start menu were scaled correctly in Kiosk mode.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1028">修复了由于 HTTP 缓存干扰以组为目标的展台模式Azure AD问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1028">Fixed an issue due to HTTP caching interfering with kiosk mode targeted to Azure AD groups.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1029">修复了在预配包中启用开发人员模式后用户无法使用"配对"按钮的问题，除非用户禁用并重新启用开发人员模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1029">Fixed an issue where users were unable to use the Pair button after enabling Developer mode with provisioning packages unless they disabled and re-enabled Developer mode.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-2004---september-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1040">Windows Holographic 版本 2004 - 2020 年 9 月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1040">Windows Holographic, version 2004 - September 2020 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1041">内部版本 19041.1117</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1041">Build 19041.1117</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1042">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1042">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1043">解决了当 appxmanifest Visual Studio SupportsMultipleInstances="true"时阻止用户调试应用程序的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1043">Addresses an issue that prevented Visual Studio from debugging an application when SupportsMultipleInstances=”true” is present in the appxmanifest.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1044">此版本包括 NCSI 代理检测修补程序，用于解决通过网络代理进行 Internet 检测失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1044">This release includes NCSI proxy detection fix to address failed Internet detection over network proxy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1045">NCSI 可以使用计算机代理和按配置文件代理进行 Internet 连接检测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1045">NCSI can use machine proxy and per-profile proxy for Internet connectivity detection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1046">NCSI 将在未来版本中支持每用户代理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1046">Per-user proxy will be supported by NCSI in future release.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1047">在大多数Windows Mixed Reality，当用户的头部处于向前的中性位置时，向前向向量与地面并行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1047">On most Windows Mixed Reality devices, the forward direction vector is parallel to the ground when the user's head is in a neutral position looking forward.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1048">但是，早期版本的 HoloLens 2使矢量与显示面板垂直，而显示面板相对于理想方向向下倾斜几度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1048">However, earlier versions of HoloLens 2 aligned the vector to be perpendicular to the display panels instead, which is tilted downward a few degrees relative to the ideal orientation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1049">较新版本的 HoloLens 2更正了此错误，以确保窗体因素之间的语义一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1049">Newer versions of HoloLens 2 have corrected this to ensure semantic consistency across form factors.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1050">改进了手部跟踪可靠度，这导致特定方案中的跟踪损失减少。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1050">Improved hand tracking robustness that will result in fewer tracking losses in specific scenarios.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1051">此版本包含一个修补程序，用于提高音频时间戳质量，这可能会导致视频捕获问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1051">This release contains a fix to improve audio timestamp quality which may have contributed to video capture issues.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1093">改进了录制视频中的全息影像稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1093">Improved hologram stability in recorded videos.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1094">解决了混合现实捕获在设备处于待机状态多天后无法录制视频的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1094">Resolved an issue where mixed reality capture couldn't record video after the device was left in standby state for multiple days.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1095">对于 Unity 应用程序，通常禁用 HolographicSpace.UserPresence API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1095">The HolographicSpace.UserPresence API is generally disabled for Unity applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1096">此行为可避免在视器翻转时导致某些应用暂停的问题，即使启用了"在后台运行"设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1096">This behavior avoids an issue that caused some apps to pause when the visor was flipped up, even if the "run in the background" setting was enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1097">现已为 Unity 版本 2018.4.18 及更高版本以及 2019.3.4 及更高版本启用 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1097">The API is now enabled for Unity versions 2018.4.18 and later and 2019.3.4 and later.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1098">通过证书设备门户访问Wi-Fi，Web 浏览器可能会由于证书无效而阻止对 的访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1098">When you access Device Portal over a Wi-Fi connection, a web browser might prevent access to due to an invalid certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1099">即使设备证书以前受信任，浏览器也可能报告"ERR_SSL_PROTOCOL_ERROR"等错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1099">The browser might report an error such as "ERR_SSL_PROTOCOL_ERROR," even if the device certificate was previously trusted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1100">在这种情况下，无法继续设备门户，因为无法忽略安全警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1100">In this case, you can't progress to Device Portal, as there's no option to ignore security warnings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1101">此更新解决了问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1101">This update resolved the issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1102">如果先前已在电脑上下载并信任设备证书以删除浏览器安全警告，并且发生 SSL 错误，则必须下载新证书并将其信任，以解决浏览器安全警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1102">If the device certificate was previously downloaded and trusted on a PC to remove browser security warnings, and the SSL error occurs, the new certificate has to be downloaded and trusted to address browser security warnings.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1103">支持创建可通过使用 .MSIX 包安装应用的运行时预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1103">Enabled the ability to create a runtime provisioning package that can install an app by using MSIX packages.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1104">添加了 **设置**  >  **系统**  >  **全息影像** 中的设置，该设置允许用户在设备关闭时自动删除混合现实主页中的所有全息影像。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1104">Added a setting in **Settings** > **System** > **Holograms** that allows users to automatically remove all holograms from Mixed Reality home when the device shuts down.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1105">修复了一个问题，该问题导致在 HoloLens 模拟器中将更改像素格式的 HoloLens 应用程序呈现为黑色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1105">Fixed an issue that caused HoloLens apps that change their pixel format to render black in the HoloLens emulator.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1106">修复了 Iris 登录期间导致崩溃的 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1106">Fixed a bug that caused a crash during Iris login.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1107">修复了有关现有应用的重复存储下载的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1107">Fixed an issue about repeated store downloads for already-current apps.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1108">修复了一个 bug，以防止沉浸式应用重复打开 Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1108">Fixed a bug to prevent immersive apps from opening Microsoft Edge repeatedly.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1109">修复了从1903版更新后初始启动时启动照片应用的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1109">Fixed an issue with launches of the Photos app in initial boots after updating from the 1903 release.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1110">提高了性能和可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1110">Improved performance and reliability.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---june-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1111">Windows 全息，版本 1903-2020 更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1111">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - June 2020 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1112">生成18362.1064</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1112">Build 18362.1064</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1113">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1113">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1114">如果未指定自定义的 MRC 录像机，则为某些属性提供新的默认值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1114">Custom MRC recorders have new default values for certain properties if they aren't specified.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1115">在 *MRC 视频效果*：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1115">On the *MRC Video Effect*:</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1116">PreferredHologramPerspective (1 PhotoVideoCamera) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1116">PreferredHologramPerspective (1 PhotoVideoCamera)</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1117">GlobalOpacityCoefficient (0.9 (HoloLens) 1.0 (沉浸式耳机) ) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1117">GlobalOpacityCoefficient (0.9 (HoloLens) 1.0 (Immersive headset))</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1118">在 " *MRC 音频" 效果* 上：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1118">On the *MRC Audio Effect*:</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1119">LoopbackGain (Windows 设备门户中混合现实捕获页面上当前的 "应用音频增益" 值) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1119">LoopbackGain (the current "App Audio Gain" value on the Mixed Reality Capture page in Windows Device Portal)</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1120">MicrophoneGain (Windows 设备门户中混合现实捕获页面上的当前 "Mic 音频增益" 值) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1120">MicrophoneGain (the current "Mic Audio Gain" value on the Mixed Reality Capture page in Windows Device Portal)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1121">对于 Unity 应用程序，通常禁用 HolographicSpace UserPresence API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1121">The HolographicSpace.UserPresence API is generally disabled for Unity applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1122">此行为可避免当面板翻转时导致某些应用暂停的问题，即使启用了在后台运行的设置也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1122">This behavior avoids an issue that causes some apps to pause when the visor is flipped up, even if the setting to run in the background is enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1123">现在为 Unity 版本2018.4.18 和更高版本以及2019.3.4 和更高版本启用了 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1123">The API is now enabled for Unity versions 2018.4.18 and later, and 2019.3.4 and later.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1124">修复了一个问题，该问题导致在 HoloLens 模拟器中将更改像素格式的 HoloLens 应用程序呈现为黑色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1124">Fixed an issue that caused HoloLens apps that change their pixel format to render black in the HoloLens Emulator.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1125">修复了从1903版更新后初始启动时启动的照片应用程序的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1125">Fixed an issue about launches of the Photos app in initial boots after updating from the 1903 release.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-2004"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1126">Windows 全息，版本2004</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1126">Windows Holographic, version 2004</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1128">适用于 HoloLens 2 的 Windows 全息版主要软件更新、 *Windows 全息版、版本 2004* 包含一种令人兴奋的新功能，例如支持 Windows Autopilot、应用程序暗模式、USB 以太网支持 5G/LTE 热点，等等。2020</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1128">The May 2020 major software update for HoloLens 2, *Windows Holographic, version 2004* includes a host of exciting new capabilities, such as support for Windows Autopilot, app dark mode, USB Ethernet support for 5G/LTE hotspots, and much more.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1129">若要更新到最新版本，请打开 "**设置**"   应用，中转到 " **更新 & 安全**"，然后选择 " **检查更新**"   按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1129">To update to the latest release, open the **Settings** app, go to **Update & Security**, and select the **Check for Updates** button.</span></span>

### <a name="support-for-windows-autopilot"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1152">支持 Windows Autopilot</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1152">Support for Windows Autopilot</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1153">Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2 允许设备销售渠道预先注册到 Intune 租户中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1153">Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2 lets the device sales channel pre-enroll HoloLens into your Intune tenant.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1154">设备到达后，它们就可以自行部署为租户下的共享设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1154">When devices arrive, they’re ready to self-deploy as shared devices under your tenant.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1155">若要利用自部署，设备必须在安装过程中的第一个屏幕上通过使用 USB 到以太网连接到网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1155">To take advantage of self-deployment, the device must connect to a network during the first screen in setup by using a USB-C-to-Ethernet.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1156">用户启动 Autopilot 自行部署过程后，此过程将完成以下步骤：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1156">After a user starts the Autopilot self-deploying process, the process completes the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1157">将设备加入到 Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1157">Join the device to Azure Active Directory (Azure AD).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1158">使用 Azure AD 在 Microsoft Intune (或其他 MDM 服务) 中注册设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1158">Use Azure AD to enroll the device in Microsoft Intune (or another MDM service).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1159">下载设备目标策略、证书和网络配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1159">Download the device-targeted policies, certificates, and networking profiles.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1160">设置设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1160">Provision the device.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1161">向用户显示登录屏幕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1161">Present the sign-in screen to the user.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1162">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Windows Autopilot For HoloLens 2 评估指南](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens2-autopilot)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1162">Learn more from the [Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2 evaluation guide](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens2-autopilot).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1163">*请联系你的帐户管理员立即加入 AutoPilot preview。即将开始交付 Autopilot 的设备。*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1163">*Contact your Account Manager to join the AutoPilot preview now. Autopilot-ready devices will begin shipping soon.*</span></span>

### <a name="fido2-security-key-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1164">FIDO2 安全密钥支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1164">FIDO2 security key support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1165">某些用户在工作或学校环境中与其他用户共享一台 HoloLens 设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1165">Some users share a HoloLens device with others in a work or school environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1166">因此，用户无需键入较长的用户名和密码，就很重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1166">So it's important that users can easily without typing long user names and passwords.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1167">快速标识在线 (FIDO) 允许组织中的任何人 (Azure AD 租户) 无需输入用户名或密码即可无缝登录到 HoloLens。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1167">Fast Identity Online (FIDO) lets anyone in your organization (Azure AD tenant) seamlessly sign-in to HoloLens without entering a user name or password.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1168">FIDO2 安全密钥是一种基于标准的无密码身份验证方法，可采用任何外形规格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1168">FIDO2 security keys are an "unphishable" standards-based passwordless authentication method that can come in any form factor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1169">FIDO 是无密码 authentication 的开放标准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1169">FIDO is an open standard for passwordless authentication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1170">它允许用户和组织无需用户名或密码即可登录到其资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1170">It allows users and organizations to sign in to their resources without a user name or password.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1171">相反，它们使用内置于设备中的外部安全密钥或平台密钥。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1171">Instead they use an external security key or a platform key built into a device.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1172">若要开始，请参阅 [Enable 无密码 security key sign in](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/authentication/howto-authentication-passwordless-security-key)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1172">To get started, see [Enable passwordless security key sign-in](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/authentication/howto-authentication-passwordless-security-key).</span></span>

### <a name="improved-mdm-enrollment-via-provisioning-package"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1173">通过预配包改进了 MDM 注册</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1173">Improved MDM enrollment via provisioning package</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1174">预配包使你可以通过配置文件而不是通过 HoloLens 全新体验来设置 HoloLens 配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1174">Provisioning packages let you set HoloLens configuration through a config file rather than through the HoloLens out-of-box experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1175">以前，必须将预配包复制到 HoloLens 内部内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1175">Previously, provisioning packages had to be copied onto the HoloLens internal memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1176">现在，它们可以位于 USB 驱动器上，因此可以更轻松地在多个 HoloLens 设备上重复使用，并且可以并行设置设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1176">Now they can be on a USB drive so they're easier to reuse on multiple HoloLens devices and you can provision devices in parallel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1177">预配包现在还支持用于在设备管理中注册的字段，因此，在预配后无手动设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1177">Provisioning packages now also support a field to enroll in device management so there's no manual setup after provisioning.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1178">试试看：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1178">To try it out:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1179">从 Windows 应用商店将最新版本的 Windows 配置设计器下载到你的电脑上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1179">Download the latest version of the Windows Configuration Designer from the Windows store onto your PC.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1180">选择 "**预配 hololens 设备**" "  >  **预配 hololens 2 设备**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1180">Select **Provision HoloLens Devices** > **Provision HoloLens 2 devices**.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1181">生成配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1181">Build your configuration profile.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1182">然后将创建的所有文件复制到 USB-C 存储设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1182">Then copy all files that were created to a USB-C storage device.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1183">将 USB-C 设备插入任何刚刷新的 HoloLens。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1183">Plug the USB-C device into any freshly flashed HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1184">然后按 **下音量**  +  **键**，以应用预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1184">Then press the **volume down** + **power** buttons to apply your provisioning package.</span></span>

### <a name="line-of-business-application-install-status"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1185">业务线应用程序安装状态</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1185">Line-of-business application install status</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1186">适用于业务线应用的 MDM 应用部署和管理对于 HoloLens 至关重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1186">MDM app deployment and management for line of business apps is critical to HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1187">管理员和用户需要查看应用安装状态以进行审核和诊断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1187">Admins and users need to view app install status for auditing and diagnosis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1188">在此版本中，我们在 **设置**  >  **帐户**  >  **访问工作或学校**  >  **单击你的帐户信息时添加了**  >  更多详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1188">In this release, we added more details in **Settings** > **Accounts** > **Access work or school** > **Click on your account** > **Info**.</span></span>

### <a name="additional-csps-and-policies"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1189">其他 Csp 和策略</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1189">Additional CSPs and policies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1190">[ (CSP) 的配置服务提供程序](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/configuration-service-provider-reference?redirectedfrom=MSDN)是一个用于读取、设置、修改或删除设备上的配置设置的接口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1190">A [configuration service provider (CSP)](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/configuration-service-provider-reference?redirectedfrom=MSDN) is an interface to read, set, modify, or delete configuration settings on a device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1191">在此版本中，我们添加了对更多策略的支持，以提高管理员对已部署的 HoloLens 设备的控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1191">In this release, we add support for more policies to increase the control administrators have over deployed HoloLens devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1192">有关 HoloLens 支持的 Csp 列表，请参阅 [NETWORKQOSPOLICY CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1192">For the list of CSPs supported by HoloLens, see [NetworkQoSPolicy CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1193">本版本中的新主题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1193">New in this release:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1194">**策略云解决方案提供商**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1194">**Policy CSP**</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1195">策略配置服务提供程序使企业能够在 Windows 设备上配置策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1195">The Policy configuration service provider enables the enterprise to configure policies on Windows devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1196">在此版本中，我们为 HoloLens 添加了新策略，这里列出了这些策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1196">In this release, we added new policies for HoloLens, which are listed here.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1197">若要了解详细信息，请参阅 [HoloLens 2 支持的策略 csp](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policies-supported-by-hololens2)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1197">To learn more, see [Policy CSPs supported by HoloLens 2](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policies-supported-by-hololens2).</span></span>  

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1198">LetAppsAccessCamera_ForceAllowTheseApps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1198">LetAppsAccessCamera_ForceAllowTheseApps</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1208">AllowWiFi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1208">AllowWiFi</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1209">**NetworkQoSPolicy 云解决方案提供商**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1209">**NetworkQoSPolicy CSP**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1210">NetworkQoSPolicy 配置服务提供程序创建 (QoS) 策略的网络服务质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1210">The NetworkQoSPolicy configuration service provider creates network quality-of-service (QoS) policies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1211">QoS 策略根据一组匹配的条件对网络流量执行一组操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1211">A QoS policy performs a set of actions on network traffic based on a set of matching conditions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1212">若要了解详细信息，请参阅 [NETWORKQOSPOLICY CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1212">To learn more, see [NetworkQoSPolicy CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp).</span></span>

### <a name="expanded-usb-ethernet-support-for-5glte-tethered-devices"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1213">为 5G/LTE 受限设备扩展 USB 以太网支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1213">Expanded USB Ethernet support for 5G/LTE tethered devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1214">添加了支持，以使某些移动宽带设备（例如 5G/LTE 手机和 Wi-Fi 热点）通过 USB 受限到 HoloLens 2 时使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1214">Support was added to enable certain mobile broadband devices, such as 5G/LTE phones and Wi-Fi hotspots, when they're tethered to the HoloLens 2 via USB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1215">这些设备现在作为另一个以太网连接显示在 " **网络设置** " 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1215">These devices are now displayed in **network settings** as another Ethernet connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1216"> (不支持需要外部驱动程序的移动宽带设备。 ) 此功能在 Wi-Fi 不可用时启用了高带宽连接，并且 Wi-Fi tethering 的性能不够高。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1216">(Mobile broadband devices that require an external driver aren't supported.) This functionality enables high-bandwidth connections when Wi-Fi is not available and Wi-Fi tethering isn't performant enough.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1217">若要了解有关受支持的 USB 设备的详细信息，请参阅 [连接到蓝牙和 USB 设备](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-connect-devices)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1217">To learn more about supported USB devices, see [Connect to Bluetooth and USB-C devices](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-connect-devices).</span></span>  

### <a name="hand-tracking-improvements"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1218">手动跟踪改进</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1218">Hand tracking improvements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1219">此版本包含多项跟踪改进：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1219">This release includes several hand tracking improvements:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1220">指示 **稳定性：** 系统现在在拒绝封闭像素时，会对索引手指进行弯曲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1220">**Pointing pose stability:** The system now resists bending the index finger when it gets occluded by the palm.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1221">当你推送按钮、类型、滚动内容和其他内容时，此更改会提高准确性！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1221">This change improves the accuracy when you push buttons, type, scroll content, and more!</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1222">**减少了意外的空中点击：** 我们改进了对 $ 攻分流手势的检测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1222">**Reduced accidental air taps:** We improved detection of the air tap gesture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1223">现在几个常见情况下的意外激活次数较少，例如，当您将指针放在您的侧面时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1223">There are now fewer accidental activations in several common scenarios, such as when you drop your hands to your sides.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1224">**用户交换机可靠性：** 当你共享设备时，系统现在更快、更可靠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1224">**User switch reliability:** The system is now faster and more reliable at updating the hand size when you share a device.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1225">**精简的手偷窃：** 我们改进了对传感器进行两次干预的情况的处理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1225">**Reduced hand stealing:** We improved handling of cases where there are more than two hands in view of the sensors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1226">如果有多个人密切合作，则现在会有很少的机会将用户从用户 "跳转" 到场景中的其他人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1226">If multiple people are working close together, there's now a much lower chance that the tracked hand will "jump" from the user to the hand of someone else in the scene.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1227">**系统可靠性：** 修复了一个问题，该问题导致手动跟踪在设备负载较高时停止工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1227">**System reliability:** Fixed an issue that caused hand tracking to stop working when the device is under high load.</span></span>

### <a name="dark-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1228">深色模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1228">Dark mode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1229">许多 Windows 应用现在支持深色和浅色模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1229">Many Windows apps now support both dark and light modes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1230">HoloLens 2 用户可以为同时支持这两种应用的应用选择默认模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1230">HoloLens 2 users can choose the default mode for apps that support both.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1231">更新之后，默认应用模式为 "深色"，但你可以轻松地更改此设置：导航到 "**设置**" "  >  **系统**  >  **颜色**" "  >  **选择默认的应用模式**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1231">After the update, the default app mode is "dark," but you can easily change this setting: Navigate to **Settings** > **System** > **Colors** > **Choose your default app mode**.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1232">这些 "内置" 应用支持暗色模式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1232">These "in-box" apps support dark mode:</span></span>

### <a name="cortana-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1248">Cortana 更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1248">Cortana updates</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1249">更新后的应用程序可与 Microsoft 365 集成，以帮助你在设备上进行更多的操作， (当前仅 US-English) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1249">The updated app integrates with Microsoft 365 to help you get more done across your devices (currently in US-English only).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1250">在 HoloLens 2 上，Cortana 不再支持某些特定于设备的命令，例如调整音量或重新启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1250">On HoloLens 2, Cortana no longer supports certain device-specific commands, like adjusting volume or restarting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1251">新的系统语音命令现在支持这些选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1251">These options are now supported by the new system voice commands.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1252">在 [博客](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2020/02/28/cortana-in-the-upcoming-windows-10-release-focused-on-your-productivity-with-enhanced-security-and-privacy/)中了解有关新 Cortana 应用的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1252">Learn more about the new Cortana app in our [blog](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2020/02/28/cortana-in-the-upcoming-windows-10-release-focused-on-your-productivity-with-enhanced-security-and-privacy/).</span></span>

### <a name="quality-improvements-and-fixes"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1253">质量改进和修复</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1253">Quality improvements and fixes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1254">更新中也有改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1254">Improvements and fixes also in the update:</span></span>  
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1255">引入了活动的显示校准系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1255">Introduced an active display calibration system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1256">此功能可改善全息影像的稳定性和对齐方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1256">This feature improves the stability and alignment of holograms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1257">当你从一侧到另一侧时，它们现在就会保持不变。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1257">They now stay in place when you move your head from side to side.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1258">修复了一个 bug，在这种情况下，Wi-Fi 流式传输到 HoloLens 会定期中断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1258">Fixed a bug where Wi-Fi streaming to HoloLens got disrupted periodically.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1259">如果应用程序指示它需要低延迟流式处理，请通过调用 [SetSocketMediaStreamingMode 函数](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/api/socketapi/nf-socketapi-setsocketmediastreamingmode)来实现修复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1259">If an application indicates that it needs low latency streaming, implement the fix by calling the [SetSocketMediaStreamingMode function](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/api/socketapi/nf-socketapi-setsocketmediastreamingmode).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1260">修复了在研究模式下流式处理期间发生的设备挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1260">Fixed a device hang that occurred during streaming in research mode.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1261">修复了一个 bug，在某些情况下，当恢复会话时，正确的用户将不会显示在登录屏幕上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1261">Fixed a bug where in some cases the right user wouldn't be displayed on the sign-in screen when resuming a session.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1262">修复了用户无法通过 **设置** 导出 MDM 日志的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1262">Fixed an issue where users couldn't export MDM logs through **Settings**.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1263">修复了在全新安装后立即进行目视跟踪的准确性可能低于预期的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1263">Fixed an issue where the accuracy of eye tracking immediately following out-of-box setup could be lower than expected.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1264">修复了在某些情况下，眼睛跟踪子系统未能初始化或执行校准的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1264">Fixed an issue where the eye tracking subsystem failed to initialize or perform calibration under certain conditions.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1265">解决了向已校准的用户提示目视校准的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1265">Fixed an issue where eye calibration would be prompted for an already-calibrated user.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1266">修复了驱动程序在目视校准过程中崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1266">Fixed an issue where a driver would crash during eye calibration.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1267">解决了重复电源按钮按下的问题可能导致60秒系统超时和 shell 崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1267">Fixed an issue where repeated power button presses could cause a 60-second system timeout and shell crash.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1268">提高了深度缓冲区的稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1268">Improved stability for depth buffers.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1269">在反馈中心添加了 " **共享** " 按钮，以便用户可以更轻松地共享反馈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1269">Added a **Share** button in the Feedback Hub so users can more easily share feedback.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1270">修复了 RoboRaid wan't 安装正确的 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1270">Fixed a bug where RoboRaid wan't installed correctly.</span></span>

### <a name="known-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1271">已知问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1271">Known issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1272">Zh-chs 系统语言的问题会阻止语音命令采用混合现实捕获或显示设备 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1272">An issue with the zh-CN system language prevents voice commands from taking a mixed reality capture or displaying the device IP address.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1273">问题要求在启动设备后启动 Cortana 应用以使用 "你好 Cortana" 语音激活。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1273">An issue requires you to launch the Cortana app after starting the device to use "Hey Cortana" voice activation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1274">如果从18362版本进行了更新，则在 **启动** 时，你可能还会看到以前版本的 Cortana 应用的第二个应用磁贴。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1274">If you updated from a 18362 build, you may also see a second app tile for the previous version of the Cortana app that no longer works in **Start**.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---may-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1275">Windows 全息，版本 1903-5 2020 月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1275">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - May 2020 Update</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1276">生成18362.1061</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1276">Build 18362.1061</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39c90-1277">这一月度质量更新不包含任何显著的更改，因为团队正在处理 Windows 全息版本2004可能会更新，如前文所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1277">This monthly quality update doesn't contain any notable changes because the team was working on the Windows Holographic version 2004 May Update, as described earlier.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---april-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="39c90-1278">Windows 全息，版本 1903-2020 更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1278">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - April 2020 Update</span></span>

UserPresence API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1309">Temporarily disabled the HolographicSpace.UserPresence API for Unity applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1310">此更改避免了在向上翻转面板时导致某些应用暂停的问题，即使启用了 "在后台运行" 设置也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1310">This change avoids an issue that caused some apps to pause when the visor was flipped up, even if the "run in the background" setting was enabled.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1311">修复了手动跟踪引起的随机 HUP 崩溃，在这种情况下，用户会注意到，在几秒钟后，UI 冻结后会返回到 shell。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1311">Fixed a random HUP crash caused by hand tracking, in which the user noticed a UI freeze then back to shell after several seconds.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1312">改善了手动跟踪，这样当你通过食指时，该手指的上半部分就不会意外地弯曲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1312">Improved hand tracking so that when you poke with your index finger, the upper part of that finger is less likely to curl unexpectedly.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="39c90-1313">提高了头跟踪、空间映射和其他运行时的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39c90-1313">Improved reliability of head tracking, spatial mapping, and other runtimes.</span></span>
